<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вставать.html>встава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вставлять.html>вставля́ть</a> (7426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вставной.html>вставно́й</a> (23316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>вста́в</a>(ить)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstáv(itʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вставной.html>вставно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstavnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> insert, insertion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вставной.html>вставны́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рама.html>ра́мы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vstavnýje</b> rámy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">double window-frames</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вставной.html>вставно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>кадр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vstavnój</b> kadr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cut-in; insert</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>plug-in</li>
<li>false, artificial <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a body part</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***встать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a> (367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">възстати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭzstati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">въз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз- / вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz- / vs-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">statʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восстать.html>восста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosstátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the Church Slavonic version of the prefix.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вставать.html>встава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand up, to get up, to rise</li>
<li>to rise <i>(sun)</i></li>
<li>to arise, to come up <i>(question)</i></li>
<li>to stop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подняться.html>подня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podnjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встревать.html>встрева́ть</a> (21654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-стрева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-strevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встревать.html>встрева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встрять.html>встрять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to meddle/intervene in</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застревать.html>застрева́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zastrevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застрять.html>застря́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zastrjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>встре<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:встрять.html>встрять</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встрепенуться.html>встрепену́ться</a> (6810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">трепе-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepe-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встрепенуться.html>встрепену́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrepenútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to rouse oneself, to start, <i>(bird)</i> to shake its wings, to open/spread its wings</li>
<li><i>(heart)</i> to throb, to beat faster</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встретивший.html>встре́тивший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrétivšij</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstréča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>meeting, encounter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ча</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rabóčaja <b>vstréča</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">workshop venue, business meeting, working-level meeting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>date</li>
<li>reception</li></ol>

***встречавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встречавший</a> (1426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrečávšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrečátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***встречаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a> (1114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrečátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstrečátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́титься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to meet, to encounter, to come across (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental case)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взор.html>взо́ры</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́тились</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ix vzóry <b>vstrétilisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">their eyes met</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднение.html>затрудне́ниями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vstrečátʹsja</b> s zatrudnénijami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to encounter difficulties</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to see each other, to meet, to date
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rédko <b>vstrečátʹsja</b> s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see little of smb.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">částo <b>vstrečátʹsja</b> s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see a good deal of smb.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be found, to be met with, to occur, to happen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rédko <b>vstrečátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be uncommon, be rare in occurrence, be a rarity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> шотла́ндии <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дикий.html>ди́кие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кошка.html>ко́шки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v Šotlándii ješčó <b>vstrečájutsja</b> díkije kóški</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wild cats are still to be found in Scotland</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstrečátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b>встре<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́титься</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-встреч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ча</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstréča</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">encounter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:встречный.html>встре́чный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vstréčnyj</b> véter</i> ― <span class="e-translation">headwind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
